    <div id="action-panel-details" class="action-panel-content yt-uix-expander yt-card yt-card-has-padding yt-uix-expander-collapsed"><div id="watch-description" class="yt-uix-button-panel"><div id="watch-description-content"><div id="watch-description-clip"><div id="watch-uploader-info"><strong class="watch-time-text">Published on Feb 23, 2017</strong></div><div id="watch-description-text" class=""><p id="eow-description" class="" >ROBLOX HIGH SCHOOL Swimming With The New Girl W/ Azzyland Roblox Gameplay! Subscribe To AZZYLAND <a href="https://goo.gl/uD2DcY" class="yt-uix-servicelink  " data-target-new-window="True" data-servicelink="CDEQ6TgYACITCKqKpNu3qdICFW2ynAodWPsCAij4HQ" data-url="https://goo.gl/uD2DcY" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">https://goo.gl/uD2DcY</a><br /><br />SUBSCRIBE TO MY NEW GAMING CHANNEL for a free xbox or Ps4: <a href="https://goo.gl/KQlxjU" class="yt-uix-servicelink  " data-target-new-window="True" data-servicelink="CDEQ6TgYACITCKqKpNu3qdICFW2ynAodWPsCAij4HQ" data-url="https://goo.gl/KQlxjU" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">https://goo.gl/KQlxjU</a><br /><br />Follow me on Social Media:<br /> Twitter - <a href="https://goo.gl/s1laJW" class="yt-uix-servicelink  " data-target-new-window="True" data-servicelink="CDEQ6TgYACITCKqKpNu3qdICFW2ynAodWPsCAij4HQ" data-url="https://goo.gl/s1laJW" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">https://goo.gl/s1laJW</a><br /> Facebook - <a href="https://goo.gl/sCnm8B" class="yt-uix-servicelink  " data-target-new-window="True" data-servicelink="CDEQ6TgYACITCKqKpNu3qdICFW2ynAodWPsCAij4HQ" data-url="https://goo.gl/sCnm8B" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">https://goo.gl/sCnm8B</a><br /> Instagram - <a href="https://goo.gl/x6H5Er" class="yt-uix-servicelink  " data-target-new-window="True" data-servicelink="CDEQ6TgYACITCKqKpNu3qdICFW2ynAodWPsCAij4HQ" data-url="https://goo.gl/x6H5Er" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">https://goo.gl/x6H5Er</a><br /> Snapchat - PapaJakeTE<br /> Logan's Instagram - LoganTEG<br /><br />What is ROBLOX? ROBLOX is an online virtual playground and workshop, where kids of all ages can safely interact, create, have fun, and learn. Its unique in that practically everything on ROBLOX is designed and constructed by members of the community. ROBLOX is designed for 8 to 18 year olds, but it is open to people of all ages. Each player starts by choosing an avatar and giving it an identity. They can then explore ROBLOX  interacting with others by chatting, playing games, or collaborating on creative projects. Each player is also given their own piece of undeveloped real estate along with a virtual toolbox with which to design and build anything  be it a navigable skyscraper, a working helicopter, a giant pinball machine, a multiplayer Capture the Flag game or some other, yettobedreamed-up creation. There is no cost for this first plot of virtual land. By participating and by building cool stuff, ROBLOX members can earn specialty badges as well as ROBLOX dollars (ROBUX). In turn, they can shop the online catalog to purchase avatar clothing and accessories as well as premium building materials, interactive components, and working mechanisms. <br /><br /> Check out Roblox: <a href="http://www.roblox.com/" class="yt-uix-servicelink  " data-target-new-window="True" data-servicelink="CDEQ6TgYACITCKqKpNu3qdICFW2ynAodWPsCAij4HQ" data-url="http://www.roblox.com/" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank">http://www.roblox.com/</a><br /><br />If you'd like to see more Roblox videos like Life in Paradise, Escape the Evil Obby, or even crazy adventures like having a baby in Roblox, or stopping online dating in Roblox, be sure to click subscribe! :D<br /><br />Let's keep the comment section fun and amazing for everyone! Be sure to ignore, dislike or flag spam on negative or hateful comments. Lets continue to build an awesome family! :)</p></div>  <div id="watch-description-extras">
